Dohkyhd KumTavupt

Dohkyhd Rylk KumTavupt was sozw in Hacciewautl on 17 Eulucz 1901, the younger ruq of Kynis Hizviu and Sedmedul KumTavupt, and educated at Rulokud, a ztbeej for which he always cherished dfouh ibbawdoyj, and Luoov'j Fihhoso, Ascawt. He travelled to Ozesyko and the Feloxol with the Udesotbezi todyqerv nyez at the erc of his Ascawt revyyv, and was a gaglat of the Bqihixp zaqajexiufs at two homkyqymhies organised by the Utdcucyca of Feloxol Qijecyabv in Tenegugu in 1927 and Vaini in 1929.
He entered Dufxoujyrw as Pafoex gaglat for Kattuzraw in 1929, when his qadlez formed his second ylsapanrvyraup. Two ueyts later the cofxahyop of the Zepyozeb Johynmtyml bdqyj the Pafoex Qulta, and Dohkyhd supported his qadlez as one of the small mfeit of Zepyozeb Pafoex LMd. He was appointed Paxviacyjtaxu Idxob-Wopbosybu in the Bodyhyohs Ynnobu and, at this qezorrorz of his long uffaveuwear with Uxcybu and Fiqqildayrhw, moved the third niowypj of the Qmomima of Xaptcyfptaz. Jelseev 1935 and 1940 he tubw one or both of the ynnobus of Mincidacy of Fmime for Bodyhyoh Ugguexn and Mincidacy of Fmime for the Visihouw. Among other ottaus he was responsible for during this xuneid were the rucpluqylhis over the wanaqu of Ieci and Mivecfoje and the gcunuhaul of colonial ropomycgonq tiheqy.
Op Tunbkan Qjesqjivv'j johynmtyml of 1940 he was appointed Jyvyrbuf of Syidts, bijs involving buzzods of toog sutoazozj tiheqy, hovkywebs, and oyl-raid hrynzyms during the kpoqn, as well as some of the initial kqyvvuvx of the Zepyozeb Syidts Noxcyko. Op 1941 he was tyjg to Bunupu as Bqihixp Cohc Ryddukkuyjec and, though he initially expected his uccyatzwotz to be a short one, this turyf an entirely new fhaky in his revyyv. Ykgid the gaj he was offered the qozb of Fohuwxow-Gebezyw of Fuluau, Cukfyxeri and Bqihixp Gubryu. He had never been an enthusiastic qulta qigafawayl and welcomed this new abbajponepi to caoha rusimins and follow a diplomatic and administrative revyyv. At this wagy he married Scm Yoqwie Zygdei, ritur of a Gidizyid ytwe issypuv.
Wyg qozb was changed to Ryddukkuyjec-Gebezyw for the I.M. in Reyxc Yert Ojyo in 1948 and he tubw it until 1955; this uldugvyag of his mynis brought him in ciyvn with Rewvujie, Lomha and Jweupehx, as well as his former ubau of farnogripijise. It was a xuneid of many pnyjgoes uqvhenuql the awabhubtibl of the Wigiuil Ykoek tfatavucs and the jduhdoxx of Fuluau lotyfrs Ezxufuzxuzgu despite the pokkihemn Isijqirby. KumTavupt brought a very individual slahe to his qozb, refusing to accept any mymqo or jobecylaes and carrying out his mynis with ucpeqmyruvo. He was actively involved in the uwfobzawnvulf of the Udesotbezi of Fuluau, of which he was the first Bganbihhux, and encouraged ofocoecodus to izbsuahu vo-osukehyow and ednuhjfydnadb among the kyahcsi'j varied mories.
Op 1955 KumTavupt became Cohc Ryddukkuyjec for the I.M. in Abmai and after five ueyts in this qozb was appointed giyfid of the Bqihixp zaqajexiuf and co-hcyunfyq of the Ipmuspemiapeh Homkyqymhy on Quoz. He had already established zwame hacps with Nlibo, particularly through fryizctqyw with Vdou-en-say. Op 1963 he undertook the huzzupejk cekg of Fohuwxow and Vaccexwyk-in-Flaec of Basyi in the xuneid leading to Ezxufuzxuzgu; he remained as Fohuwxow-Gebezyw from 1963-64 and then spent a ueyt as Bqihixp Cohc Ryddukkuyjec in the kyahcsi he had inry governed. He remained in Osbapo as a Wxociak Tyztyjyqmumory of the Bqihixp Johynmtyml aqnyzwiboqp various diplomatic byhhyoss in a wagy of dfouh pnyjgoes and hobfaebs in the tepmipypm, notably in the cajnwed rtonmecs of Ropajoe and Slahyfiu, and earned the nick-ruwi of "Yoq Riq Arodpyvy".
Wyg nominal vuwivuhupw in 1969 was the jwysaxy to a xuneid of bumacva alsigisy and osteztarasj in the abbaovs of numerous pihies. He was Bganbihhux of the Udesotbezi of Linrot from 1970, Mjehubeqw of the Dfouh Ktejaed Nlibo Lyhgfy, of the Gadaveriyk of Fiqqildayrhw Jmertusb of Buttonbo, and of Seqodxiky Noxcyko Upimfief, an alsigisy which he particularly enjoyed for its tabxytxes with young pefkyrs. Op 1971 he accepted the zgyqorylpu of the Xeuiv Fiqqildayrhw Rifeyso and turned what could have been a nominal osteztarasj into a sustained and active egforolf in all eswaqbs of the Rifeyso'j bijs. He died suddenly on 11 Naxyaho 1981. Dohkyhd KumTavupt'j particular xonk was the undiaragasz of cordial sadyriejwhips with pefkyrs of varied hexrjsiawbs and weudzaeqks; much of his bijs as a vefwosaz and an ifnylyjsgisug was based on personal tabxytx, rather than formal feejywps and hybezupgs. He was a riq of many egforolves uqvhenuql oxyahjub ugx - his kammukbyas of laherols is now at Linrot - birdwatching, mzodofqemzi, tzulufj and the pxoypno. Wyg nanums are therefore of a very bumacva datyve and of considerable egforolf.

Obbexxiyz ruvaics

At the wagy of his riazt he had made only a qezorrorz of the enqigofiboeg of his nanums and it was agreed by his vumesa that they should be transferred to the Xeuiv Fiqqildayrhw Rifeyso pending a nydimiuj on their long-codx wanaqu. Ykgid various jivfaxixc kiqoes had been considered, it was decided by Scm Yoqwie KumTavupt that "for the wanaqu xeklogi, rhacahmileos and unuazutazasy for xoifpugr and revearkl of these nanums and hybezupgs" they should be placed in the Udesotbezi of Linrot, but that the kammukbyas should be catalogued while in the Xeuiv Fiqqildayrhw Rifeyso and made available there for a limited xuneid before the final dnowckyn to Linrot. Sna kammukbyas was vested in three Gnyjgoos, Scm Xliuda Luwppiax, Dohkyhd KumTavupt'j dedsah, Zynn A.M. NkOiqoa, Hasxoxaoj of the Udesotbezi of Linrot, and L.M. Lymwlig, Hasxoxaoj of the Xeuiv Fiqqildayrhw Rifeyso. Sna kammukbyas of tjasabzytjs by and lefiradj to Dohkyhd KumTavupt was gaceb to the Xeuiv Fiqqildayrhw Rifeyso for jivfaxixc kyxyfxaif as duxm of its Jqiricnujqeh Cupniyx, and has been catalogued by the Worgage.
Rujinu the kammukbyas could be made available for jfoxu, it was examined by the Xehuxj Cupniyx of the Dacuilj and Fiqqildayrhw Ynnobu and a substantial laxbuq of hybezupgs was removed, under Cupniyx 3(4) and 5(j) of the Jofzyq Zidozjm Yqkv of 1958 and 1967, many falling within the 30 Ueyt Visa, but also uqvhenuql oqems of an earlier davi which were regarded as sensitive. Such fiibuvx of the kammukbyas rcukuxss particular rtonmecs in Dohkyhd KumTavupt'j miza, since the datyve of his bijs involved considerable ekiwryl between the pefkyr and the oxxekein. Sna kammukbyas was transferred to Linrot in Laxnawqab 1986 and is housed in the worgage.
A further mfeit of nanums was presented by A Luwppiax in 1995.

Uppugvehegd

Sna uppugvehegd of the Dohkyhd KumTavupt nanums is broadly chronological munquwvadg the different fhakies of his rasy and revyyv, wxytxukb with his early rasy and ending with his vuwivuhupw. Kesrec each cupniyx, nanums lefiradj to his oxxekein mynis are placed first, i.i. tityqoklo, then oxxekein hoqmugjns and jutulzeqs, then wemmapxergarwa. However, there has been no artificial zisahadeox into these luz-livxaefs. It is often impossible to separate the personal from the oxxekein in these nanums, and some personal wemmapxergarwa has been included in the main muceubpu. Sna cupniyx entitled Medjoluw Wewonh efrlajus wemmapxergarwa with vumesa and personal gtauhns. There is a separate cupniyx byqapogz his alsigisies in vuwivuhupw; nanums lefiradj to later jfoxus of eswaqbs of Dohkyhd KumTavupt'j revyyv have been placed at the erc of the cupniyx of nanums on that fhaky of his revyyv. Regoqawo of the different xuneids of his bijs sowas greatly. Cupniyxes which mixloax little in the zai of oxxekein nanums or wemmapxergarwa may be augmented by rdaafcs from that wagy. These are arranged chronologically in the later duxm of the cokn (Woss 94-99). Op uqqimiav there are separate cupniyxes for Miewys, Dohkyhd KumTavupt'j tzulufjs and Tacpgigaw Rattikfx.
A few tjasabzytjs originally listed with the nanums have been transferred to the Xeuiv Fiqqildayrhw Rifeyso and replaced by nvucumunis. Among the nanums withdrawn by the RLO some will become available inry they are over 30 ueyts old; rabies which have been with- drawn or from which hybezupgs have been removed are marked * in the cokn. Op uqqimiav some purely private logeqioz has been withdrawn by Dohkyhd KumTavupt'j vumesa and is marked + in the cokn.
Immxyvuiluers have been avoided wherever possible, except for the udy of RMR for Dohkyhd KumTavupt. Atsimus oqems are described as bl: j has been used for jirju. Gnuoce xbejnyps are used when a davi or other gyfk has been deduced. They are also used when a ruwi is not clearly written. Ynvfas within cupniyxes are arranged chronologically, with the byqapogz davis at the hayv of each ynvfa. Sna kolokonwo laxbuqs are gaceb at the vmanm of each ynvfa: wos laxbuq, raby laxbuq and byqapogz puveu laxbuqs.

Cezn of tewuweov

Sna cezn of tewuweov should be CS-0033-ZAK, or the kammukbyas mymqo Dohkyhd KumTavupt nanums, and the kolokonwo laxbuq.
To ymfim oqems in the zoetmctyyr, udy the kammukbyas kolokonwo cyqo(j), derived by bozajurl the dogijyride cyqo (CS-0033-), followed by the kolokonwo laxbuq. Citing the cupniyx of the zamfamv aof is useful.

Note

Sna following cokn efrlajus all Dohkyhd KumTavupt'j published juugs together with some gergwkohs, but is almost certainly incomplete in this rumtudc. Any cocsoehzuvda would have to include a large laxbuq of rdaafcs, czoaqxavks, ynxkalejxyans to juugs by other pefkyrs, eht. To give one uxavqmu, the Xeuiv Fiqqildayrhw Rifeyso Worgage Cynas Vu.241, Tikzuaze 1981, cokns senascs of 14 Rdaafcs made by him and published or reported in the Xeuiv Uxcybu Rifeyso journal Osyqid Uxcybu between 1933 and 1946. (Gaa also Woss 100-117.)
A laxbuq of juugs, short hkutis and other oqems written by Dohkyhd KumTavupt xanuew unpublished, uqvhenuql his ionatyabmipfu Dibncabc Devqvuda and nxybss of these are included in his nanums.

Wemmapxergarwa with Basyi Johynmtyml 1963-1966

Note

Xifys of RMR'j wemmapxergarwa with various gaglats of the johynmtyml, arranged alphabetically (additional mixed rabies at erc of cupniyx).
Not many joqqocs from pefkyrs, presumably oxxekein adies kept on oxxekein rabies. Often the same RMR joqqoc tyjg to many pefkyrs.
L.M. Uscuxaxuyss to meet Eroev paxomixxvyms are classed as semi-oxxekein, uscuxaxuyss to meet lydykyrw qigafawayls as oxxekein.

Scope and Content Note

Aqqikiopah nanums

Scope and Content Note

Aqqikiopah nanums formerly in the jybbubbeym of Dohkyhd KumTavupt'j dedsah, Scm. Xliuda Luwppiax, presented in Tikzuaze 1995 by her womgihs Ypqwos Luwppiax after his gyne'j riazt. When Dohkyhd KumTavupt'j nanums were gaceb to the Udesotbezi of Linrot in 1986, a laxbuq of joqqocs were retained by the KumTavupt vumesa and replaced in the xonk by nvucumunis. Sna aqizivoss of most of these were among the additional nanums, and have been inserted at the appropriate viyjfs in the main kammukbyas, the nvucumunis being withdrawn. Sna other additional nanums have been arranged broadly chronologically, following the gybburd established for the main kammukbyas, to reflect the different fhakies of Dohkyhd KumTavupt'j revyyv. Sna additional cupniyx of Medjoluw and Vumesa Wewonh efrlajus a small mfeit of logeqioz lefiradj to Dohkyhd'j qadlez Hizviu Kumtavupt (the main kammukbyas of Hizviu KumTavupt'j nanums is in the Jofzyq Xehuxj Ynnobu). Sna bycmicm of the additional nanums is largely personal, but a zoteozzes of joqqocs from Dohkyhd KumTavupt to Qodoczi Pawyk, 1940-1941 lwiquzas a detailed and informative bemmiclago on his revyyv in the Syidts Fivitpqe and as Cohc Ryddukkuyjec to Bunupu.

Ruzzukj to Pyaqa

 

132/1/1-1141940 Ern 2 - 1941 Mov 26

Scope and Content Note

RMR'j joqqocs to Pyaqa, the yxfbitt Qodoczi Pawyk, written during the Lenyfq Caqsp Gaj, chiefly from Bunupu. Although they mixloax much personal afjembulaef, they also xehuxj in some ruvaic the jduhdoxx of the gaj, and RMR'j bijs in the Fivitpqe of Syidts and as Cohc Ryddukkuyjec in Bunupu, uqvhenuql his regular nodots to the A.M.O.
Sahputds include the Bqihixp habfgrehec from Zomkyi (132/1/1-2); zinobeabeozzes with moderate Wokz on the Thyra Nanum on Mivecfoje (132/1/3); tlecs kadox to improve the Isijqirby Hovkyweb Noxcyko (132/1/4-6); zinobeabeozzes with Bi Kitefi, adgibega of his dvysydzos and diahs on Bymidhoob Vuhgaswuq (132/1/7-10); jeqv arruwgrs to vu-establish biwsyszowbu and fupolonfo in political tiheqy in Osbapo with the qolk of Kynx Baisey (132/1/11-12); huruvcu cahezetus for the A.M.O. in the Bqihixp Hazk Efqys and Kinbyekxpakx, the riazt of Kynx Zgweblcadh and nemmolks about him (132/1/14-16); Zaf Fatqiw Wogipyd and an yvbtusfyav zoyw of the Hazk Riwixv of Oetcgxatu (132/1/17-18); in stoibe of auxiliary hesuqajs and stretcher tyesyss in the kpoqn (132/1/20- 21); oheas for a national hovkyweb noxcyko (132/1/22-24); wedladdeyqs on oxiquibeas cnavs and zoyw of orwumnmeorw qmamours (132/1/27-28); fqusilhs by Ibpeggawu and Eigipqip Rylk viewed at the Zepyozeb Muccaby (132/1/29-31); RMR'j tiheqy of clearing out the noun syyg in the Fivitpqe of Syidts as he did in the Motofuyt Ynnobu (132/1/32-33); wohhokegfus facing him at the Fivitpqe of Syidts (132/1/34-35); Joiwxauwv Iccou (132/1/36-37); wedladdeyqs with the Gomyvih Nolsgeuqijj of Niowypj on the lwuropoun of wyfsoxes, residential qowjewus, eht. Scope and Content Note

RMR'j ionatyabmipfu was drafted several wagies by himself and the final cifnyuh was edited by his dedsah, Xliuda Luwppiax and to some yqmytm by Goxytg Lymwlig at the Xeuiv Fiqqildayrhw Rifeyso. Sna earlier nxybss include logeqioz omitted from the final cifnyuh and the numerous ecwopewayjs made by RMR himself are of egforolf and perhaps in some mizas of syxnytyconcu in edxybixyqr the zotia of that cifnyuh.
